padding: 0 6px;'><strong><span style="color: #007576">O</span></strong></td></tr></table><p>Understanding the type of enzyme inhibition or activation is crucial for developing effective drugs and understanding metabolic regulation.</p><strong>enzyme 1</strong> converts substrate <strong><span style="color: #6c6c00">K</span></strong> into product <strong><span style="color: #3b7600">L</span></strong>. <p>The end product <strong><span style="color: #007576">O</span></strong> of this pathway binds to <strong>enzyme 1</strong>and its substrate in the active site at the same time.</p><p>This binding <strong><span style="color: brown">decreases</span></strong> the activity of the enzyme.</p><p>Determine the type of enzyme inhibition or activation described:</p>	enzyme activator	Incorrect	competitive inhibitor	Incorrect	un-competitive inhibitor	Correct	molecular stopper	Incorrect	non-competitive inhibitor	Incorrect
